# Next Steps

Scaffold define MVP shape, but real impl work ahead. Next phase: replace placeholders w/ Claude-hook-aware, model-backed, blocking behavior. Keep control flow explicit, file-backed.

## Current Priorities

1. Fix QA UX for real Claude Code hook use.
2. Upgrade competence model beyond flat score tracking.

Current UX direction:
- `/dev/tty` path is not viable in Claude Code hooks.
- Current per-question Gradio launch path is too slow + fragile.
- Near-term decision is sidecar-style QA UI with careful lifecycle management.
- UI transport still open: persistent Gradio sidecar if fastest, or lighter custom sidecar if Gradio overhead stays too high.

Current competence-model direction:
- Near-term: retrieval-backed context, not full graph-first rewrite.
- Start simple: recent interactions, recency-weighted retrieval, locality to changed code, docs/examples for relevant language/library features.
- Next step after simple retrieval: embedding similarity over prior interactions + materials.
- Stretch direction: graph/ontology-based tutoring model if time allows.

## Priority Order

1. Hook payload fidelity + mutation normalization
2. Real knowledge gate model integration
3. QA loop scoring, persistence, user interaction hardening
4. Integration tests + end-to-end local verification

## Workstreams For Four People

### Person 1: Claude Hook + Mutation Interface

Own Claude-facing interception path in `hooks/` and normalization seam in `core/normalize.py`.

Scope:
- Replace scaffold payload assumptions w/ real Claude Code `PreToolUse` payload shape.
- Enumerate day-one mutation tools, document how each maps into `ChangeProposal`.
- Improve old/new content capture for `Write`, `Edit`, `MultiEdit`, other supported mutation tools.
- Add repo-local note discovery + relevant transcript extraction inputs for context aggregation.
- Confirm emitted `allow`/`deny` contract matches Claude hook expectations.

Deliverables:
- Real payload parser in `hooks/stdin_payload.py`
- Supported mutation-tool matrix in `hooks/README.md`
- Fixture-driven tests per supported mutation shape in `tests/test_normalize.py`
- Hook integration tests in `tests/test_pre_tool_use.py`

Definition of done:
- Can feed real/recorded Claude hook payloads into `hooks/pre_tool_use.py`, get stable valid decisions.

### Person 2: Knowledge Gate + Model Adapter

Own real evaluator path in `core/gate.py` and `core/llm_adapter.py`.

Scope:
- Choose first shipping evaluator provider + model.
- Use MCP-backed docs before wiring LangChain or provider APIs.
- Replace deterministic scaffold gate w/ structured-output model evaluation.
- Enforce schema validation for `GateDecision`, fail loudly on malformed model output.
- Keep gate adapter thin so domain models stay independent from provider objects.

Deliverables:
- Real adapter impl in `core/llm_adapter.py`
- Prompting + structured-output handling for `GateDecision`
- Retry/error policy for transient provider failures
- Mock-based tests for valid, invalid, partial model responses in `tests/test_gate.py`

Definition of done:
- Gate returns spec-shaped `allow`/`block` decisions from real model, degrades clearly when provider fails.

### Person 3: QA Loop + Competence Updates

Own blocked-path teaching loop in `qa/` and competence update rules in `core/competence_store.py` + `qa/competence_updates.py`.

Scope:
- Replace heuristic answer eval w/ better mechanism-focused scoring.
- Improve adaptive retry so follow-up questions more scaffolded after failure.
- Persist pending/results artifacts in audit-friendly shape.
- Tighten competence update policy for first-pass success, retry success, fail-limit continuation.
- Replace broken hook-time terminal assumptions with sidecar-based user interaction.
- Keep renderer choice open until persistent sidecar lifecycle is proven.

Deliverables:
- Better eval logic in `qa/evaluation.py`
- Richer retry/question adaptation in `qa/question_generation.py`
- Finalized result artifact shape in `state/qa/results/`
- Expanded QA tests: pass-first-try, pass-after-retry, fail-3x in `tests/test_qa_loop.py`

Definition of done:
- Blocked change goes through full 1-3 attempt loop w/ consistent scoring + competence updates.

### Person 4: End-to-End Reliability + Local UX

Own integration quality, state ergonomics, optional UI readiness.

Scope:
- Build realistic e2e tests: hook -> gate -> QA -> state persistence.
- Improve event logging in `state/logs/events.jsonl` for debuggability.
- Add local dev commands + workflow notes for replaying intercepted payloads.
- Validate persistent sidecar QA flow for real hook usage.
- Keep Gradio optional; do not assume it is final UX surface.
- Document sidecar lifecycle rules clearly if hook flow depends on it.
- Keep docs current as architecture assumptions become concrete.

Deliverables:
- Integration-style tests for representative allow/block flows
- Event logging helpers + log assertions
- Developer workflow docs in `README.md` or dedicated local-dev doc
- Sidecar lifecycle + replay docs for local verification
- Optional renderer wiring once sidecar contract stable

Definition of done:
- Teammate can locally replay realistic flow, inspect artifacts under `state/`, understand what happened without reading source.

## Cross-Cutting Agreements

- Preserve MVP boundary: one agent, one synchronous gate, one blocking QA loop.
- Keep persisted artifacts human-readable.
- No LangGraph or hidden orchestration state.
- Prefer small modules + explicit boundaries over convenience abstractions.
- Update `AGENTS.md` + `README.md` when canonical workflow changes.

## Suggested Sequence

1. Person 1 locks down real Claude payload + mutation normalization.
2. Person 2 wires actual gate model once normalized packet stable.
3. Person 3 hardens QA eval + competence updates against real gate output.
4. Person 4 stitches flow together w/ replay tooling, logs, docs, sidecar UX validation, and clear lifecycle rules.

## Handoff Points

- Person 1 -> Person 2: finalized `ChangeProposal` + aggregated context contract
- Person 2 -> Person 3: stable `GateDecision` + `QAPacket` schema from real model output
- Person 3 -> Person 4: stable QA result artifacts + competence update semantics
- Person 4 -> everyone: replay harness, integration tests, debug workflow

File: docs/specs/graph_competence_model.md

# Spec: Graph-Based Competence Model

**Status:** Stretch proposal — not near-term default. Need team review before impl.
**Author:** Auto-generated from deep-research + plan Phase 6.
**Affects:** `core/models.py`, `core/competence_store.py`, `qa/competence_updates.py`

---

## Problem

Current competence model = flat dict concept → score. Lacks:
1. **Prerequisite relationships** — no way express `async_programming` depends on `functions` and `error_handling`.
2. **Evidence-based scoring** — scores updated by additive deltas, no time decay or audit trail weighting.
3. **Semantic concept resolution** — gate encounters new concept name, no structure to determine if maps to existing node.

## Near-Term Sequence

Before graph model work, current priority is retrieval-backed competence context.

Suggested order:
1. Retrieve recent interactions + QA outcomes.
2. Weight retrieval by recency.
3. Weight retrieval by locality to changed files/code areas.
4. Retrieve docs/examples for relevant language features, syntax, objects, libraries touched by current change.
5. Add embedding similarity over prior interactions + learning materials.
6. Revisit graph model only if simpler retrieval path proves too weak.

This doc describes longer-range direction, not recommended first implementation slice.

## Proposed Changes

### 1. Prerequisite Edges in YAML

Add optional `prerequisites` key to each concept in `competence_model.yaml`:

```yaml
concepts:
  functions:
    score: 0.7
    notes: []
    evidence: [...]
    prerequisites: [variables_and_types, control_flow]
  error_handling:
    score: 0.4
    notes: []
    evidence: [...]
    prerequisites: [functions]
```

**Backward compatibility:** Models w/o `prerequisites` keys load w/ empty lists. No migration needed — field purely additive.

### 2. NetworkX DiGraph for Prerequisite Reasoning

Build `networkx.DiGraph` from competence model on load. Edges run prerequisite → dependent (e.g., `functions → error_handling`).

Use cases:
- **Ancestor lookup** — `nx.ancestors(G, "async_programming")` → `{functions, error_handling, variables_and_types, control_flow}`
- **Learning frontier** — concepts where all prereqs score ≥ threshold but concept itself scores low
- **Weak prerequisite detection** — concept scores well but prereq doesn't, flag gap
- **Relevant subgraph extraction** — for gate prompts, extract only relevant concepts+edges (token-efficient)

### 3. Evidence-Based Scoring with Time Decay

Replace additive `delta` scoring with:

```python
def compute_score(evidence: list[CompetenceEvidence], half_life_days: float = 30.0) -> float:
    if not evidence:
        return 0.5  # prior
    now = datetime.now(UTC)
    weighted_sum = 0.0
    weight_total = 0.0
    for ev in evidence:
        age_days = (now - parse_iso(ev.timestamp)).total_seconds() / 86400
        weight = math.exp(-0.693 * age_days / half_life_days)
        outcome_value = OUTCOME_VALUES[ev.outcome]
        weighted_sum += weight * outcome_value
        weight_total += weight
    return weighted_sum / weight_total if weight_total > 0 else 0.5
```

**Outcome values:**
| Outcome | Value |
|---------|-------|
| `pass_first_try` | 1.0 |
| `pass_after_2` | 0.7 |
| `pass_after_3` | 0.5 |
| `fail_limit_reached` | 0.1 |
| `self_assessment` | mapped from 1-5 slider |

**Half-life:** 30 days default. Recent evidence dominates; old fades.

### 4. LLM-Assisted Concept Matching (Post-MVP)

Gate finds concept not in model:
1. Exact match → use existing node
2. Normalized match (lowercase + underscore) → use existing node
3. LLM query: "Is concept X semantically equivalent to any of [existing concepts]?" → map or create
4. If creating: LLM suggests prereq edges to existing concepts

Deferred until basic graph model validated.

## Data Model Changes

### `CompetenceEntry` additions

```python
@dataclass(slots=True)
class CompetenceEntry:
    score: float
    notes: list[str] = field(default_factory=list)
    evidence: list[CompetenceEvidence] = field(default_factory=list)
    prerequisites: list[str] = field(default_factory=list)  # NEW
```

### New helper: `build_concept_graph`

```python
def build_concept_graph(model: CompetenceModel) -> nx.DiGraph:
    G = nx.DiGraph()
    for name, entry in model.concepts.items():
        G.add_node(name, score=entry.score, category=...)
        for prereq in entry.prerequisites:
            G.add_edge(prereq, name)
    return G
```

### Score computation changes

`competence_store.update_competence_entry` currently applies `delta`:
```python
entry.score = min(1.0, max(0.0, round(entry.score + delta, 2)))
```

Proposed: Remove delta-based scoring. Instead:
- Always append evidence
- Compute `entry.score` on read via `compute_score(entry.evidence)`
- `score` field in YAML = cached snapshot (updated on write)

## Migration Path

1. Existing models load w/o `prerequisites` — empty list default
2. Running `vibecheck cm init` creates model w/ prereqs from taxonomy
3. `compute_score` = pure addition — existing evidence lists work unchanged
4. Delta-based `update_competence_entry` replaced, but append-evidence pattern already exists in `competence_updates.py`

## Files Modified (When Approved)

| File | Change |
|------|--------|
| `core/models.py` | Add `prerequisites` field to `CompetenceEntry` |
| `core/competence_store.py` | Add `build_concept_graph()`, modify score computation |
| `qa/competence_updates.py` | Replace delta with evidence-only appends |
| `pyproject.toml` | Promote `networkx` from optional to core dependency |

## Open Questions

1. Half-life configurable per-concept or global?
2. Prereq edges mutable via QA loop, or only explicit user action?
3. Persist computed score in YAML (current approach) or compute purely on read?

## Decision Required

Spec proposes changes to core scoring mechanism. Impl should not proceed until team reviewed+approved. `networkx` dependency already available as optional extra (`pip install 'vibecheck[graph]'`) for experimentation.


================================================
File: qa/init_survey.py
================================================
"""Gradio-based competence model initialization survey.

Presents concept sliders for self-assessment, then writes the initial
competence model YAML.
"""

from __future__ import annotations

import contextlib
import importlib
import queue
import threading
from datetime import UTC, datetime
from pathlib import Path
from typing import Any

from core.competence_store import save_competence_model
from core.concept_taxonomy import ConceptDefinition, load_taxonomy
from core.models import CompetenceEntry, CompetenceEvidence, CompetenceModel

_TIMEOUT_SECONDS = 300  # 5 minutes

# Slider value (1-5) → initial competence score (0.0-1.0)
_SCORE_MAP: dict[int, float] = {1: 0.1, 2: 0.3, 3: 0.5, 4: 0.7, 5: 0.9}


def run_gradio_survey(
    output_path: Path,
    taxonomy: list[ConceptDefinition] | None = None,
) -> CompetenceModel | None:
    """Launch the Gradio survey and return the seeded model, or None on timeout."""
    try:
        gr = _import_gradio()
    except ImportError as exc:
        raise RuntimeError(
            "Gradio is not installed. Install with: uv pip install 'vibecheck[ui]'"
        ) from exc

    concepts = taxonomy or load_taxonomy()
    result_q: queue.Queue[dict[str, int]] = queue.Queue()

    app = _build_app(gr, concepts, result_q)
    server_thread = threading.Thread(target=_launch_app, args=(app,), daemon=True)
    server_thread.start()

    try:
        ratings = result_q.get(timeout=_TIMEOUT_SECONDS)
    except queue.Empty:
        _close_app(app)
        return None
    finally:
        _close_app(app)

    model = _build_model(concepts, ratings)
    save_competence_model(model, output_path)
    return model


def _build_app(
    gr: Any,
    concepts: list[ConceptDefinition],
    result_q: queue.Queue[dict[str, int]],
) -> Any:
    with gr.Blocks(title="VibeCheck Setup", theme=gr.themes.Soft()) as app:
        gr.Markdown(
            "## VibeCheck — Competence Model Setup\n"
            "Rate your confidence with each concept below.\n"
            "**1** = No experience · **5** = Very confident"
        )

        sliders: list[Any] = []
        for concept in concepts:
            label = concept.name.replace("_", " ").title()
            s = gr.Slider(
                minimum=1,
                maximum=5,
                step=1,
                value=3,
                label=f"{label}  ({concept.category})",
            )
            sliders.append(s)

        submit_btn = gr.Button("Submit", variant="primary")
        status_text = gr.Markdown("")

        def on_submit(*slider_values: float) -> str:
            ratings = {concepts[i].name: int(v) for i, v in enumerate(slider_values)}
            result_q.put(ratings)
            return "Competence model saved. You can close this window."

        submit_btn.click(
            fn=on_submit,
            inputs=sliders,
            outputs=[status_text],
        )

    return app


def _build_model(
    concepts: list[ConceptDefinition],
    ratings: dict[str, int],
) -> CompetenceModel:
    now = datetime.now(UTC).replace(microsecond=0).isoformat().replace("+00:00", "Z")
    entries: dict[str, CompetenceEntry] = {}
    for concept in concepts:
        raw_rating = ratings.get(concept.name, 3)
        score = _SCORE_MAP.get(raw_rating, 0.5)
        entries[concept.name] = CompetenceEntry(
            score=score,
            notes=[],
            evidence=[
                CompetenceEvidence(
                    timestamp=now,
                    outcome="self_assessment",
                    note=f"User rated {raw_rating}/5",
                )
            ],
        )
    return CompetenceModel(user_id="local_default", updated_at=now, concepts=entries)


def _launch_app(app: Any) -> None:
    with contextlib.suppress(Exception):
        app.launch(share=False, quiet=True, prevent_thread_lock=True)


def _close_app(app: Any) -> None:
    with contextlib.suppress(Exception):
        app.close()


def _import_gradio() -> Any:
    return importlib.import_module("gradio")
